    exit 0; \
fi; \
if test -f \
    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/bn.xml" ; then \
        xml_derived_option="--xml-derived /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/bn.xml"; \
        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"bn" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/bn.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-bn.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/bn.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-bn.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-bn.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-bn.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-bn.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-bn.dict"; \
fi;

    exit 0; \
fi; \
if test -f \
    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/es_US.xml" ; then \
        xml_derived_option="--xml-derived /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/es_US.xml"; \
        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"es_US" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/es_US.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-es_US.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/es_US.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-es_US.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-es_US.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-es_US.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-es_US.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-es_US.dict"; \
fi;

    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/id.xml" ; then \

        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"id" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/id.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-id.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/id.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-id.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-id.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-id.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-id.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-id.dict"; \
fi;

if test -f dicts/emoji-mr.dict; then \

    exit 0; \
fi; \
if test -f \
    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/mr.xml" ; then \
        xml_derived_option="--xml-derived /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/mr.xml"; \
        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"mr" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/mr.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-mr.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/mr.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-mr.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-mr.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-mr.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-mr.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-mr.dict"; \
fi;

    exit 0; \
fi; \
if test -f \
    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/sat.xml" ; then \
        xml_derived_option="--xml-derived /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/sat.xml"; \
        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"sat" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/sat.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-sat.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/sat.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-sat.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-sat.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-sat.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-sat.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-sat.dict"; \
fi;

    exit 0; \

if test -f \
    "/usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/sw_KE.xml" ; then \
        xml_derived_option="--xml-derived /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/../annotationsDerived/sw_KE.xml"; \
        plus_comment="derived"; \
fi; \
is_skip=0; \
if test x"sw_KE" = xen ; then \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/sw_KE.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --xml-ascii ../data/annotations/en_ascii.xml \
        --out-category ibusemojigen.h \
        --out dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict; \
else \
    ./emoji-parser \
        --unicode-emoji-dir /usr/share/unicode/emoji \
        --xml /usr/share/unicode/cldr/common/annotations/sw_KE.xml \
        $xml_derived_option \
        --out dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict; \
    retval=$?; \
    if test $retval -eq 99 ; then \
        is_skip=1; \
        touch dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict; \
    elif test $retval -ne 0 ; then \
        echo "Fail to generate dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict"; \
        abrt; \
    fi; \
fi; \
if test $is_skip -eq 0 ; then \
    echo "Generated $plus_comment dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict"; \
else \
    echo "Skip $plus_comment dicts/emoji-sw_KE.dict"; \
fi;
